9. = -1/32*sin(2*(4*x - 4)) + 3/128*sin(4*(4*x - 4)) - 1/96*sin(6*(4*x - 4)) + 1/512*sin(8*(4*x - 4)) + 1/16*x + C
10. Simplify.
= -1/32*sin(8*x - 8) + 3/128*sin(16*x - 16) - 1/96*sin(24*x - 24) + 1/512*sin(32*x - 32) + 1/16*x + C

8. Simplify.
